docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:.. _`udf cuda`:
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:LiberTEM can use CUDA devices through `CuPy <https://cupy.dev/>`_. Since
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:its main processing can likely be ported to use both CPUs and CUDA devices in
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:good CUDA math library support such as large Fourier transforms or matrix
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:'cupy')` or :code:`('cupy',)`, a UDF activates being run on both CUDA and CPU
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:workers, or exclusively on CUDA workers. Using :code:`cuda` instead of
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst::code:`cupy` schedules on CUDA workers, but without using the CuPy library. This
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:is useful for running code that uses CUDA in a different way, for example
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:integration of C++ CUDA code, and allows to skip installation of CuPy in this
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:that use the same code for CUDA and CPU processing.
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:A UDF should only use one GPU at a time. If :code:`cupy` is used, the correct
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:the UDF itself. If :code:`cuda` is used, it is the responsibility of the user to
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst::meth:`libertem.common.backend.get_use_cuda`. The environment variable
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst::code:`CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES` can be set `before` any CUDA library is loaded to
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst::code:`backends` attribute to :code:`('numpy',)` :code:`('cupy',)` or :code:`('cuda',)` to
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:restrict execution to CPU-only or CUDA-only on a hybrid cluster. This is mostly
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:As an extension of :ref:`udf cuda`, LiberTEM also supports supplying UDFs with
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:tiles in sparse array formats for both CPU and GPU. A UDF specifies the
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:device class so that :ref:`udf cuda` works analogously for both dense and sparse
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst:formats. Dense CPU and GPU arrays are specified with the backends described in
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst::ref:`udf cuda` so that the extension to sparse arrays is backwards-compatible.
docs/source/udf/advanced.rst::attr:`~libertem.udf.base.UDF.BACKEND_CUDA`,
